## FAQ Draft

   Answer guidance: Give a reflective answer that combines personal context, emotion, and symbolic tradition without claiming one universal meaning.

   Answer guidance: Avoid binary certainty. Explain that tone, context, and the dreamer waking life change the interpretation.

   Answer guidance: Treat spiritual meaning as optional reflection, not doctrine or prediction.

   Answer guidance: Mention crystals as journaling or intention-setting supports, not medical or spiritual promises.

   Answer guidance: No. Dream interpretation is reflective content, not medical, mental-health, religious, legal, or financial advice.
